UV Coverage

Single dish UV coverage is according to Equation 34 in (Rodrıguez-Fernández et al., 2008).

ωVpvuv∝exp(−u2+v2d2)

where

d2=2ln(2)λ2π2θ2sd

the θsd is the beam size of the single dish telescope.

C Band

X Band

Plot code of UV coverage

C Band 

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from mpl_toolkits.axes_grid1 import make_axes_locatable
import os as os
import matplotlib.ticker as mtick

def sduv(
    beamsize,
    uvdist):
    beamsize_rad = beamsize/60./180.*np.pi #arcmin->rad
    d_sqr = (1*np.log(2.0))/(np.pi**2*beamsize_rad**2)
    return np.exp(-1*(uvdist*1e3)**2/d_sqr)

def plotuv(
              inputfile,
              outputfile
              ):
    import os as os
    plt.figure(figsize=(8,6))
    plt.rc('text', usetex=True)
    plt.rc('font', family='serif', size=10)
    f = open(inputfile,'r') 
    lines = f.readlines()
    #if os.path.isfile(outputfile):
    #   os.remove(outputfile)
    uvdist = []
    amp = []
    sduvdist = np.arange(0.01,1000.0,0.01)
    for i in range(len(lines)):
        line = lines[i].strip()
        col = line.split()
        uvdist.append(float(col[0])/1e3)
        amp.append(float(col[1]))
    ax3 = plt.subplot(211)
    ax4 = plt.subplot(212)
    ax1 = ax3.twinx()
    ax2 = ax4.twinx()
    bins = range(1, 200)
    plt.subplots_adjust(hspace = .001)
    ax1.set_xlim(0.1, 200)
    ax1.set_xscale("log")
    ax1.set_yscale("linear")
    ax1.axes.xaxis.set_ticklabels([])
    mybins = 10 ** np.linspace(np.log10(1), np.log10(200), 50)
    ax1.hist(
        (uvdist), 
        log=False, 
        bins= mybins,
        lw = 0,
        alpha = 0.4,
        color = 'g')
    ax3.text(0.5, 1.04, 
        'VLA CnB Config. C Band 5081-5083  MHz', 
        color = 'w',
        bbox={'facecolor':'g', 'alpha':0.6, 'pad':5})
    ax3.text(2.05, 0.9, 
        '--------  $\qquad$ GBT C Band', 
        color = 'r',
        bbox={'facecolor':'w', 'alpha':0.7, 'pad':5})
    ax3.plot(sduvdist,sduv(2.5,sduvdist),color = 'r')
    ax3.set_ylim(-0.12, 1.2)
    ax3.set_ylabel('GBT Beam Pattern')
    ax1.set_ylim(-5000, 50000)
    #ax1.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mtick.FormatStrFormatter('%.1f'))
    ax1.set_xlim(0.1, 200)
    ax1.set_ylabel('Number')

    #=============================================

    ax2.set_xlim(0.1, 200)
    ax2.set_ylim(-1.7, 17)
    ax4.set_ylim(-0.125, 1.25)
    ax4.set_xlim(0.1, 200)  
    ax2.set_xscale("log")
    ax2.xaxis.set_major_formatter(mtick.FormatStrFormatter('%.1f'))
    ax2.scatter(uvdist,amp, 
        s = 0.5, 
        color = 'b', 
        alpha = 0.1,
        lw = 0)
    ax4.set_xlabel('UV Distance ($10^3\ \lambda$)')
    ax2.set_ylabel('Amplitude (Jy/beam)')
    ax4.set_ylabel('GBT Beam Pattern')
    p1 = plt.Rectangle((0, 0), 0.1, 0.1, fc='b',alpha = 0.1)
    ax2.text(5.3, 15, 
        'VLA CnB Config. C Band 5081-5083  MHz', 
        color = 'w',
        bbox={'facecolor':'blue', 'alpha':0.7, 'pad':5})
    ax2.text(22, 13, 
        '--------  $\qquad$ GBT C Band', 
        color = 'r',
        bbox={'facecolor':'w', 'alpha':0.7, 'pad':5})

    #============================================

    ax4.plot(sduvdist,sduv(2.5,sduvdist),color = 'r')
    print sduv(2.5,sduvdist)
    plt.savefig(outputfile)     
    return 0

plotuv('c_10_51-53_uv.dat','c_10_51-53_uv.png')

X Band

    d_sqr = (1*np.log(2.0))/(np.pi**2*beamsize_rad**2)

        s = 0.5, 
        color = 'b', 
        alpha = 0.1,
        lw = 0)
    ax4.set_xlabel('UV Distance ($10^3\ \lambda$)')
    ax2.set_ylabel('Amplitude (Jy/beam)')
    ax4.set_ylabel('GBT Beam Pattern')
    p1 = plt.Rectangle((0, 0), 0.1, 0.1, fc='b',alpha = 0.1)
    ax2.text(5.3, 15, 
        'VLA CnB Config. X Band 9081-9083  MHz',

    ax4.plot(sduvdist,sduv(1.5,sduvdist),color = 'r')

To be insertedin the proposal

import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from mpl_toolkits.axes_grid1 import make_axes_locatable
import os as os
import matplotlib.ticker as mtick

def sduv(
    beamsize,
    uvdist):
    beamsize_rad = beamsize/60./180.*np.pi #arcmin->rad
    d_sqr = (1*np.log(2.0))/(np.pi**2*beamsize_rad**2)
    return np.exp(-1*(uvdist*1e3)**2/d_sqr)

def plotuv(
              inputfile_a,
              inputfile_b,
              outputfile
              ):
    import os as os
    plt.figure(figsize=(8,6))
    plt.rc('text', usetex=True)
    plt.rc('font', family='sans serif', size=12)
    f = open(inputfile_a,'r') 
    lines = f.readlines()
    #if os.path.isfile(outputfile):
    #   os.remove(outputfile)
    uvdist = []
    amp = []
    sduvdist = np.arange(0.01,1000.0,0.01)
    for i in range(len(lines)):
        line = lines[i].strip()
        col = line.split()
        uvdist.append(float(col[0])/1e3)
        amp.append(float(col[1]))
    ax1 = plt.subplot(211)
    ax2 = plt.subplot(212)
    ax3 = ax1.twinx()
    ax4 = ax2.twinx()
    plt.subplots_adjust(hspace = .001)
    ax1.set_xlim(0.2, 200)
    ax1.set_ylim(-1.7, 17)
    ax3.set_ylim(-8000, 80000)
    ax1.set_xscale("log")
    ax1.xaxis.set_major_formatter(mtick.FormatStrFormatter('%.1f'))
    #ax3.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mtick.FormatStrFormatter('%i'%))
    vals = ax3.get_yticks()
    ax3.set_yticklabels(['{:3.0f}'.format(x/1e4) for x in vals])
    ax1.scatter(uvdist,amp, 
        s = 5, 
        color = 'grey', 
        alpha = 0.1,
        lw = 0,
        rasterized=True)
    #ax1.set_xlabel('UV Distance ($10^3\ \lambda$)')
    ax1.set_ylabel('Amplitude (Jy/beam)')
    ax3.set_ylabel('Data Points /$10^4$')
    p1 = plt.Rectangle((0, 0), 0.1, 0.1, fc='b',alpha = 0.1)
    ax1.text(0.25, 15, 
        'VLA CnB Config. C Band 5081-5083  MHz', 
        color = 'w',
        bbox={'facecolor':'grey', 'alpha':0.85, 'pad':5},
        size = 12)
    mybins = 10 ** np.linspace(np.log10(1), np.log10(200), 50)
    ax3.hist(
        (uvdist), 
        log=False, 
        bins= mybins,
        lw = 1.2,
        alpha = 1,
        color = 'k',
        fc='None')
    ax1.axhline(y=0.0,color = 'k')
    ax1.axvspan(0, 1.6, ymin=1.7/18.7, ymax=0.3, alpha=0.6, color='red',lw = 0)
    ax1.text(0.5, 1.3, 
        'GBT', 
        color = 'w',
        size=15)
    ax1.axvspan(0.58, 16.7, ymin=0.3, ymax=0.5, alpha=0.6, color = 'blue',lw = 0)
    ax1.text(1.3, 5.28, 
        'VLA D Config.', 
        color = 'w',
        size=15)
    ax1.axvspan(11.3, 600.0, ymin=0.5, ymax=0.7, alpha=0.6, color = 'green',lw = 0)
    ax1.text(25, 9.02, 
        'VLA A Config.', 
        color = 'w',
        size=15)

    #=============================================

    f = open(inputfile_b,'r') 
    lines = f.readlines()
    #if os.path.isfile(outputfile):
    #   os.remove(outputfile)
    uvdist = []
    amp = []
    sduvdist = np.arange(0.01,1000.0,0.01)
    for i in range(len(lines)):
        line = lines[i].strip()
        col = line.split()
        uvdist.append(float(col[0])/1e3)
        amp.append(float(col[1]))

    ax2.set_xlim(0.2, 200)
    ax2.set_ylim(-1.7, 17)
    ax4.set_ylim(-8000, 80000)
    ax2.set_xscale("log")
    ax2.xaxis.set_major_formatter(mtick.FormatStrFormatter('%.1f'))
    #ax4.yaxis.set_major_formatter(mtick.FormatStrFormatter('%i'%))
    vals = ax4.get_yticks()
    ax4.set_yticklabels(['{:3.0f}'.format(x/1e4) for x in vals])
    ax2.scatter(uvdist,amp, 
        s = 5, 
        color = 'grey', 
        alpha = 0.1,
        lw = 0,
        rasterized=True)
    ax2.set_xlabel('UV Distance ($10^3\ \lambda$)')
    ax2.set_ylabel('Amplitude (Jy/beam)')
    ax4.set_ylabel('Data Points /$10^4$')
    p1 = plt.Rectangle((0, 0), 0.1, 0.1, fc='b',alpha = 0.1)
    ax2.text(0.25, 15, 
        'VLA CnB Config. X Band 9081-9083  MHz', 
        color = 'w',
        bbox={'facecolor':'grey', 'alpha':0.85, 'pad':5},
        size = 12)
    mybins = 10 ** np.linspace(np.log10(1), np.log10(200), 50)
    ax4.hist(
        (uvdist), 
        log=False, 
        bins= mybins,
        lw = 1.2,
        alpha = 1,
        color = 'k',
        fc='None')
    ax2.axhline(y=0.0,color = 'k')
    ax2.axvspan(0, 2.88, ymin=1.7/18.7, ymax=0.3, alpha=0.6, color='red',lw = 0)
    ax2.text(0.5*1.2, 1.3, 
        'GBT', 
        color = 'w',
        size=15)
    ax2.axvspan(1.044, 30.06, ymin=0.3, ymax=0.5, alpha=0.6, color = 'blue',lw = 0)
    ax2.text(1.3*1.8, 5.28, 
        'VLA D Config.', 
        color = 'w',
        size=15)
    ax2.axvspan(20.34, 1080, ymin=0.5, ymax=0.7, alpha=0.6, color = 'green',lw = 0)
    ax2.text(25*1.2, 9.02, 
        'VLA A Config.', 
        color = 'w',
        size=15)
    #============================================

    print sduv(2.5,sduvdist)
    plt.savefig(outputfile)     
    return 0

plotuv('c_10_51-53_uv.dat','x_10_51-53_uv.dat','c_10_51-53_uv_shaded.png')
